Master Level 5
Description Summons Mihile to strike down multiple enemies with four powerful blows. Skill level can be increased depending on your level.

Active Mihile's Soul
Master Level 10
Description Summons a spirit that automatically performs an area attack on the enemies you are fighting. Skill level increases by 1 every 15 levels.
Level 1 MP Cost: 11, Damage: 70%, Duration: 110 sec
The damage of Ultimate Explorer minion skills is calculated differently from that of the character.
10 MP Cost: 20, Damage: 160%, Duration: 200 sec
The damage of Ultimate Explorer minion skills is calculated differently from that of the character.

Show/hide all levels
Passive Invincible Belief
Master Level 6
Description Muster your faith in the darkest of times to recover health.
Does not activate in towns or while affected by statuses that prevent HP recovery. Not affected by effects which reset cooldowns, increase buff durations, or modify recovery skill potency.
This Link Skill can be stacked up to 3 times, once for each unique Explorer Warrior job character you have on this world.
Level 1 Automatically activates when your health falls to 15% of your Max HP or below. Restores 20% of Max HP every 1 sec for 3 sec
Cooldown: 410 sec.
6 Automatically activates when your health falls to 15% of your Max HP or below. Restores 35% of Max HP every 1 sec for 3 sec
Cooldown: 210 sec.

Active Leap Attack
Master Level 1
Description Ambush the enemy by rapidly dropping to ground from mid-air.
Can only be used if there's a platform within range below you. Use along with a left or right arrow keys to drop yourself diagonally.
Can also be used by pressing the downward, left, or right arrow keys plus the attack key, instead of manually activating the skill.
Level 1 MP Cost: 5, Damage: 90%, Number of Attacks: 2, Max Enemies Hit: 4

Active Evil Eye
Master Level 1
Description Summons an Evil Eye, which heals you regularly when it is near. Can be toggled On/Off.
Level 1 Casts heal that restores 20 HP every 24 sec.
Show/hide all levels
Active Evil Eye Shock
Master Level 10
Description The Evil Eye releases a terrifying scream that deals damage to nearby enemies.
Not affected by attack reflection.
Unlocks Evil Eye Shock II at Level 10.
Level 1 The Evil Eye appears in front of you, attacking up to 10 enemies 6 times, dealing 123% damage with a 9% chance of stunning targets for 5 sec.
Cooldown: 12 sec.
10 The Evil Eye appears in front of you, attacking up to 10 enemies 6 times, dealing 150% damage with a 45% chance of stunning targets for 5 sec.
Cooldown: 12 sec.

Passive Final Attack
Master Level 20
Description Chance to deliver an additional hit after a direct attack skill. Must have a Spear or Polearm weapon equipped.
Required Skill: Weapon Mastery Lv. 3
Level 1 [Final Attack Skill] Has a 2% chance to deal a final attack that deals 61% damage 2 time(s).
20 [Final Attack Skill] Has a 40% chance to deal a final attack that deals 80% damage 2 time(s).

Description Accept the contract with the darkness. If HP becomes 0 while a selected pact is in effect, Final Pact will be activated. Cannot trigger while Final Pact is on cooldown.

Required Skill: Final Pact Lv. 1
Level 1 Use the arrows key within 5 sec. of using this skill to select the type of pact you want to accept.
Cooldown: 1 sec
Show/hide all levels
Passive Final Pact
Master Level 30
Description When your HP reaches 0, your dark contract keeps you alive, granting invincibility based on the type selected in Accept Final Pact. Additionally, if you eliminate and successfully attack the required number of monsters for a set period of time after invincibility ends, cooldown will be reduced until the next contract.
Not affected by cooldown reset. When HP is above a certain amount, permanently increases Final Damage, Speed, Critical Rate, and Critical Damage.
Level 1 Fully restores your HP and MP when the effect activates. Invincibility effect activates based on the type selected in Final Pact Accept.
Final Pact Quarter: Invincibility Duration: 2 sec. Cooldown will shorten by 70 sec. if you defeat 24 enemies or attack a boss during the 10 sec. after invincibility activates.
Cooldown: 383 sec.
Final Pact Half: Invincibility Duration: 8 sec. Cooldown will shorten by 80 sec. if you defeat 44 enemies or attack a boss during the 20 sec. after invincibility activates
Cooldown: 463 sec.
Final Pact Full: Invincibility Duration: 40 sec. Cooldown will shorten by 300 sec. if you defeat 52 enemies or attack a boss during the 40 sec. after invincibility activates
Cooldown: 1103 sec.
[Passive Effects: When HP is 78% or above, Final Damage: +1%, Speed: +6, Critical Rate: +1%, Critical Damage: +5%]
30 Fully restores your HP and MP when the effect activates. Invincibility effect activates based on the type selected in Final Pact Accept.

Cooldown: 180 sec.

Cooldown: 260 sec.
Final Pact Full: Invincibility Duration: 40 sec. Cooldown will shorten by 300 sec. if you defeat 52 enemies or attack a boss during the 40 sec. after invincibility activates
Cooldown: 900 sec.
[Passive Effects: When HP is 20% or above, Final Damage: +30%, Speed: +20, Critical Rate: +10%, Critical Damage: +15%]

Master Level 25
Description Collect Erda from within yourself and from the surrounding area, then detonate it around your enemies. The Erda of attacked enemies will become disrupted, which will bind their movements. Can deal damage to enemies even when they are under Attack Ignore. Also ignores Attack Reflection.

Active Erda Shower
Master Level 25
Description Fires a blast of compressed Erdas at nearby enemies.
Pressing the skill key with the down arrow key summons an Erda Fountain, an object filled with pure Erda.
With Action Customization enabled, you can summon Erda Fountain by pressing its skill key again, without the use of the arrow keys.
Right-click to toggle Action Customization ON/OFF
Level 1 HP Cost: 3000
Erdas Shower
Max Enemies Hit: 15, Damage: 465%, Number of Attacks: 6, Cooldown reduced by 2 sec per attacked enemy
Cooldown: 40 sec
Erda Fountain
Object Summon Duration: 60 sec. Every time enemies in a map with the summoned object are defeated, the Erda released from the enemies condenses around the object.
Defeating 12 or more will release the gathered Erda, Max Enemies Hit: 10, Damage: 465%, Number of Attacks: 4
Cooldown: 60 sec
Cooldown shared with Erdas Shower and Erda Fountain.

Active Blitz Shield
Master Level 25
Description Harnesses your own Lifeforce to create a protective shield. You can detonate this shield to inflict damage to nearby enemies.
Level 1 HP Cost: 5% of Max HP, Creates a protective shield, absorbing damage up to 15% of your Max HP for 5 sec.
If you activate this skill a second time, it detonates and inflicts 520% damage to 12 enemies 5 times.
Your shield must be active for at least 2 sec before it can be detonated.
Cooldown: 15 sec

Master Level 25
Description Infuses your weapon with a portion of your health, granting it a visible aura and temporarily empowering it. The aura wave is unaffected by attack reflection. Affected by effects which reduce cooldown.

Active Calamitous Cyclone
Master Level 25
Description Swings a spear so fast it creates a dark storm and devastate the area in front of you. The final attack is unaffected by attack ignore and attack reflection.
Level 1 MP Cost: 100. Deals 394% damage 8 times consecutively, on up to 12 enemies, for up to 4 sec. Recover 1% of max HP for every attack that lands. Attacks up to 26 times.
When key is released, activates a shockwave 8 times that deals 15 final attack(s) with 801% damage to a max of 12 enemies. Recover 10% of max HP for every final attack that lands.
All Calamitous Cyclone hits receive Additional Critical Rate: +100%, and Additional Monster Def Ignored: +50%
Cooldown: 180 sec.

Active Darkness Aura
Master Level 25
Description By the power of the enhanced contract with darkness, unleash a dark aura to both siphon enemies' life force and add a special ability.
Darkness Aura is unaffected by Attack Reflection. Reusing this skill during its effect will offer the absorbed life force to darkness, allowing you to make a deadly attack. During the final attack of Gungnir's Descent, Nightshade Explosion, and Calamitous Cyclone, it is possible to cancel the final detonation.
Level 1 MP Cost: 1000. Periodically attack up to 3 enemies for 416% damage 5 times over 40 sec. Recover 3% Max HP per attack and obtain 1 Life Force. If HP Recovery exceeds Max HP, gain an HP shield amounting to 75% of the recovery amount. Max Life Force: 10, Max Shield: 15% of Max HP. Periodically generates a maximum-strength shield. Damage Taken -4% (includes damage proportional to Max HP).
Reusing this skill can instantly trigger a dark slash that strikes 8 enemies for 625% damage 13 times, plus an additional 1 slashes for each 1 Life Force possessed.
Cooldown: 180 sec.
25 MP Cost: 1000. Periodically attack up to 3 enemies for 800% damage 5 times over 40 sec. Recover 3% Max HP per attack and obtain 1 Life Force. If HP Recovery exceeds Max HP, gain an HP shield amounting to 75% of the recovery amount. Max Life Force: 10, Max Shield: 27% of Max HP. Periodically generates a maximum-strength shield. Damage Taken -9% (includes damage proportional to Max HP).
Reusing this skill can instantly trigger a dark slash that strikes 8 enemies for 1225% damage 13 times, plus an additional 1 slashes for each 1 Life Force possessed.
Cooldown: 180 sec.
30 MP Cost: 1000. Periodically attack up to 3 enemies for 880% damage 5 times over 40 sec. Recover 3% Max HP per attack and obtain 1 Life Force. If HP Recovery exceeds Max HP, gain an HP shield amounting to 75% of the recovery amount. Max Life Force: 10, Max Shield: 30% of Max HP. Periodically generates a maximum-strength shield. Damage Taken -10% (includes damage proportional to Max HP).
Reusing this skill can instantly trigger a dark slash that strikes 8 enemies for 1350% damage 13 times, plus an additional 1 slashes for each 1 Life Force possessed.
Cooldown: 180 sec.

Mastery Skills

Active HEXA Gungnir's Descent
Master Level 30
Description Throws a mythical spear to deal fatal damage. It deals greater damage when you have greater Max HP.
Required Skill: Gungnir's Descent Lv. 30
Level 1 MP Cost: 60, Damage: 245%, Max Enemies Hit: 4, Number of Attacks: 12
When Attacking: Damage increases by 120% of Max HP for every attack, Enemy Defense Ignored: 31%.
30 MP Cost: 70, Damage: 390%, Max Enemies Hit: 4, Number of Attacks: 12
When Attacking: Damage increases by 120% of Max HP for every attack, Enemy Defense Ignored: 40%.

Enhancements

Enhancements require the corresponding V Skill to be leveled to max and equipped. Final Damage bonuses from Enhancements increase linearly each level, with a jump at levels 10, 20, and 30.
